  <script>
   // Google Maps Form Autocomplete API
	
		var placeSearch, autocomplete, autocomplete2, form1, form2;
		var componentMapping = {
			street_number: '.form-row.address1 input',
			route: '.form-row.address1 input',
			locality: '.form-row.city input',
			administrative_area_level_1: '.form-row.states select,.form-row.state select',
			administrative_area_level_3: '.form-row.city input',
			country: '.form-row.country select',
			postal_code: '.form-row.postal-code input,.form-row.zip input'
		};

		var componentForm = {
			street_number: 'short_name',
			route: 'long_name',
			locality: 'long_name',
			administrative_area_level_1: 'short_name',
			administrative_area_level_3: 'short_name',
			country: 'short_name',
			postal_code: 'short_name'
		};

		function initAutocomplete() {
			form1 = $($('.form-row.address1 input')[0]).closest('form');
			form2 = $($('.form-row.address1 input')[1]).closest('form');
			if (form1.length > 0) {
				autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete((form1.find('.form-row.address1 input')[0]), {
					types: ['geocode']
				});
				autocomplete.addListener('place_changed', fillInAddress);
			}
			if (form2.length > 0) {
				autocomplete2 = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete((form2.find('.form-row.address1 input')[0]), {
					types: ['geocode']
				});
				autocomplete2.addListener('place_changed', fillInAddress2);
			}

			$('.form-row.address1 input').attr('autocomplete','on');
		}

		function fillInAddress() {
			var street = '';
			var place = autocomplete.getPlace();
			for (var component in componentForm) {
				form1.find(componentMapping[component]).val('')
			}
			for (var i = 0; i < place.address_components.length; i++) {
				var addressType = place.address_components[i].types[0];
				if (componentForm[addressType]) {
					var val = place.address_components[i][componentForm[addressType]];
					var theInput = form1.find(componentMapping[addressType]);
					
					if (addressType == 'street_number' || addressType == 'route') {
						if (street != '') {
							street = street + ' ';							
						}
						street = street + val;
						if (addressType == 'route') {
							theInput.val(street);
						}
					} else {
						theInput.val(val);
					}
					
					if (addressType != 'street_number') {
						if( theInput.val().trim() !== '' ) { // foro yoshiko effect
							$(theInput.parentNode).addClass( 'input--filled' );
						}						
					}
				}
			}

			form1.find('select[name$="_addressFields_countries_country"]').trigger('change');
			$('select').selectric('refresh');
		}

		function fillInAddress2() {
			var street = '';
			var place = autocomplete2.getPlace();
			for (var component in componentForm) {
				form2.find(componentMapping[component]).val('')
			}
			for (var i = 0; i < place.address_components.length; i++) {
				var addressType = place.address_components[i].types[0];
				if (componentForm[addressType]) {
					var val = place.address_components[i][componentForm[addressType]];
					var theInput = form2.find(componentMapping[addressType]);
					
					if (addressType == 'street_number' || addressType == 'route') {
						if (street != '') {
							street = street + ' ';							
						}
						street = street + val;
						if (addressType == 'route') {
							theInput.val(street);
						}
					} else {
						theInput.val(val);
					}
					
					if (addressType != 'street_number') {
						if( theInput.val().trim() !== '' ) { // foro yoshiko effect
							$(theInput.parentNode).addClass( 'input--filled' );
						}						
					}
				}
			}
			form2.find('select[name$="_addressFields_countries_country"]').trigger('change');
			$('select').selectric('refresh');
		}

		function geolocate() {
			if (navigator.geolocation) {
				navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(position) {
					var geolocation = {
						lat: position.coords.latitude,
						lng: position.coords.longitude
					};
					var circle = new google.maps.Circle({
						center: geolocation,
						radius: position.coords.accuracy
					});
					autocomplete.setBounds(circle.getBounds())
				})
			}
		}
		$(document).ready(function () {
			$('.form-row.address1 input').on("focus", function() {
				geolocate();
				$(this).attr('autocomplete','off');
				
			}).on("blur", function() {
				$(this).attr('autocomplete','on');
			});
		});
  </script>
  <script defer="" src="https://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?key=AIzaSyAFOUIcZ-qOBTWN7hqEbbYilXOiYQApALI&amp;libraries=places&amp;callback=initAutocomplete">
  </script>

	var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
	for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {
	  var c = ca[i];
	  while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);

  <script>
   var cdnUrlVar = 'https://www.katvondbeauty.com/dw/image/v2/AAXW_PRD/on/demandware.static/-/Sites-KVD-Library/default/v1529608637947/';
	function cdnUrl(){
		$('*[background-cdn]').each(function() {$(this).css('background-image',('url("'+cdnUrlVar + $(this).attr('background-cdn')+'")'));});	
		$('img[src-cdn]').each(function() {
			if ($(this).attr('src-cdn').indexOf('ytimg') > -1) {$(this).attr('data-src', $(this).attr('src-cdn')).removeAttr("src-cdn").addClass('lazyload');}
			else {$(this).attr('data-src',(cdnUrlVar + $(this).attr('src-cdn'))).removeAttr("src-cdn").addClass('lazyload');}
		});}

	        return true;

	    try {
	        var _stsi1 = setInterval(function () {
	            if (!window.jQuery) { return; }
	            clearInterval(_stsi1);
	            if (typeof id == "undefined" || id == "") { return; }

   <script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
	/* Used to reset the activity tracker parameters in the pdict upon successful send up to Listrak endpoint. */
	function resetProductActivityParams()
	{
		var path = '/on/demandware.store/Sites-KVD-Site/default/ltkActivityTrackerClearItems-ClearFlag';
		jQuery.ajax({
			  url: path,
			  context: document,
			  success: function(){ }
		});
	}	
	
	try {
		/* Perform activity/page/product browse logging. */
		var sessionSku = 'null';
		var sessionCategory = 'null';
		var sessionQuickViewSkus = 'null';		
		
		/* Iterate through any quickviews and add them as product browses. */
		if (sessionQuickViewSkus != null && sessionQuickViewSkus != "null" && sessionQuickViewSkus.length > 0)
		{
			var quickViews = sessionQuickViewSkus.split(',');
			
			for (var i = 0; i < quickViews.length; i++)
			{
				_ltk.Activity.AddProductBrowse(quickViews[i]);			
			}
		}
		
		/* Add the product browse if we have it. */
		if (sessionSku != null && sessionSku != "null" && sessionSku.length > 0)
		{
			_ltk.Activity.AddProductBrowse(sessionSku);
		}			
		
		/* Add the page browse. We should ALWAYS have if this JS fires. */
		var currentPage = window.location.href;
		_ltk.Activity.AddPageBrowse(currentPage);
		
		/* Submit the activity through client side JS to the endpoint. */
		_ltk.Activity.Submit();
		
		/* Do a post to reset the browse/quickview/page parameters if there are products in them. */
		resetProductActivityParams();
	}
	catch (er)
	{
		/* An error has occurred, yet to determine if we want to do anything here. */
	}
});

<script>
	// Google Maps Form Autocomplete API
	
		var placeSearch, autocomplete, autocomplete2, form1, form2;
		var componentMapping = {
			street_number: '.form-row.address1 input',
			route: '.form-row.address1 input',
			locality: '.form-row.city input',
			administrative_area_level_1: '.form-row.states select,.form-row.state select',
			administrative_area_level_3: '.form-row.city input',
			country: '.form-row.country select',
			postal_code: '.form-row.postal-code input,.form-row.zip input'
		};

		var componentForm = {
			street_number: 'short_name',
			route: 'long_name',
			locality: 'long_name',
			administrative_area_level_1: 'short_name',
			administrative_area_level_3: 'short_name',
			country: 'short_name',
			postal_code: 'short_name'
		};

		function initAutocomplete() {
			form1 = $($('.form-row.address1 input')[0]).closest('form');
			form2 = $($('.form-row.address1 input')[1]).closest('form');
			if (form1.length > 0) {
				autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete((form1.find('.form-row.address1 input')[0]), {
					types: ['geocode']
				});
				autocomplete.addListener('place_changed', fillInAddress);
			}
			if (form2.length > 0) {
				autocomplete2 = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete((form2.find('.form-row.address1 input')[0]), {
					types: ['geocode']
				});
				autocomplete2.addListener('place_changed', fillInAddress2);
			}

			$('.form-row.address1 input').attr('autocomplete','on');
		}

		function fillInAddress() {
			var street = '';
			var place = autocomplete.getPlace();
			for (var component in componentForm) {
				form1.find(componentMapping[component]).val('')
			}
			for (var i = 0; i < place.address_components.length; i++) {
				var addressType = place.address_components[i].types[0];
				if (componentForm[addressType]) {
					var val = place.address_components[i][componentForm[addressType]];
					var theInput = form1.find(componentMapping[addressType]);
					
					if (addressType == 'street_number' || addressType == 'route') {
						if (street != '') {
							street = street + ' ';							
						}
						street = street + val;
						if (addressType == 'route') {
							theInput.val(street);
						}
					} else {
						theInput.val(val);
					}
					
					if (addressType != 'street_number') {
						if( theInput.val().trim() !== '' ) { // foro yoshiko effect
							$(theInput.parentNode).addClass( 'input--filled' );
						}						
					}
				}
			}

			form1.find('select[name$="_addressFields_countries_country"]').trigger('change');
			$('select').selectric('refresh');
		}

		function fillInAddress2() {
			var street = '';
			var place = autocomplete2.getPlace();
			for (var component in componentForm) {
				form2.find(componentMapping[component]).val('')
			}
			for (var i = 0; i < place.address_components.length; i++) {
				var addressType = place.address_components[i].types[0];
				if (componentForm[addressType]) {
					var val = place.address_components[i][componentForm[addressType]];
					var theInput = form2.find(componentMapping[addressType]);
					
					if (addressType == 'street_number' || addressType == 'route') {
						if (street != '') {
							street = street + ' ';							
						}
						street = street + val;
						if (addressType == 'route') {
							theInput.val(street);
						}
					} else {
						theInput.val(val);
					}
					
					if (addressType != 'street_number') {
						if( theInput.val().trim() !== '' ) { // foro yoshiko effect
							$(theInput.parentNode).addClass( 'input--filled' );
						}						
					}
				}
			}
			form2.find('select[name$="_addressFields_countries_country"]').trigger('change');
			$('select').selectric('refresh');
		}

		function geolocate() {
			if (navigator.geolocation) {
				navigator.geolocation.getCurrentPosition(function(position) {
					var geolocation = {
						lat: position.coords.latitude,
						lng: position.coords.longitude
					};
					var circle = new google.maps.Circle({
						center: geolocation,
						radius: position.coords.accuracy
					});
					autocomplete.setBounds(circle.getBounds())
				})
			}
		}
		$(document).ready(function () {
			$('.form-row.address1 input').on("focus", function() {
				geolocate();
				$(this).attr('autocomplete','off');
				
			}).on("blur", function() {
				$(this).attr('autocomplete','on');
			});
		});

	
</script>


	<script defer src="https://maps.googleapis.com/maps/api/js?key=AIzaSyAFOUIcZ-qOBTWN7hqEbbYilXOiYQApALI&libraries=places&callback=initAutocomplete" ></script>
